info:Guestroom - with View (2 beds)
info:Stayed in December 2021
info:Family
info:7 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted December 27, 2021
msg:I love Yiqinyuan for the calm and peaceful forest, I walked by myself during the last day and if you do visit, try to do it without any gadget. Just bring your keycard. Walk through the tall trees, hear the birds, feel the sun and inhale fresh air.

It is very sad that I have a non-refundable ticket that made me not enjoy the accomodation I booked. Since it was the coldest day of the year they decided to move all guests who stays in the container van rooms to their building rooms. To move  In their main building I need to add more payment and we were relocated to building 5. It was also an advantage since the Foresta Cafe was there and the playroom (not so much in there but still worth the visit). However, the room we were in was so dusty, the aircon was blowing some dusty air and the carpet was so dirty. It ruined the whole trip and even of they were able to change the beddings and vacuum the carpet it was still tickling our noses. We were really looking forward to a nice Christmas trip but yeah. I booked 3 nights because we really love the place. üò≠ The next day I asked again to be moved to a different room, they said they were fully booked but alas there was an available room next to us. The first room was so inconvenient because whenever we turn the lights off the WIFI also goes off. The fridge was not working well, the temperature outside was much better. The second room was better than the first room but the exhaust fan wasn't working. 

The breakfast was only located in the main restaurant which was 15 mins (waiting for the electric car) away from our building. It was a race to get to breakfast and the seating was not enough to be near the buffet. Time is running and you have Marathon between your table and the buffet table. Food was great though they alternate between the dates. Dinner was also good and had great service but not so much choice of small dished for a small family. Local food at it's best!

La Foresta Cafe was interesting. They helped us keep our Christmas pies in their fridge. The only way to order was via the QR on the table but the catch was you have to pay right away for your order to go through which waa different from the main restaurant. So there we were waiting for our food but they didn't really get through and had to end up sitting and waiting for an hour. The next day it took 30 mins. for the food to come. The taste was good serving was big, can share.

The electric cars were very prompt and the drivers were very kind and polite.

The food again was really yummy!

The staff were friendly too.

You can buy swan/duck feed at 5rmb/2 packs at the coffee shop at the reception. 

They were giving away eyemask and heatpacks.
The bottles water was also free. The snack at the room was cheaper than the vending machine.

It is far from the town so make sure you have what you need before heading to the resort.

They have hangers and iron in every room at building 5 where we stayed. 

Not a lot of English speaking staff so bring some Mandarin phrases or get ready with a translator APP.

After a long mixed review I just wish that the resort informed us ahead that the accomodation will not be available and made an option for rebooking or ensure better accomodation it was really a hassle.

msg:The main purpose of this trip to Chongming is to go bird watching in Dongtan and Xisha. This hotel is located on the south side of the Forest Park. It occupies a large area with lush forests and crisscrossing water systems. The hotel facilities are satisfactory, the environment is beautiful, and it is especially rich in bird resources. In addition to the black swans and mallards that are stocked in the hotel, there are also many wild small grebes on the lake. While walking around, I observed the types of forest birds including sparrows, magpies, blackbirds, white wagtails, pearl-necked doves, mountain doves, black-tailed grosbeaks, grey-headed buntings, white-headed bulbuls, northern redstarts and common kingfishers.

You need to apply for them at the front desk of the guest room center when checking in. The TV in the room was turned on for a long time, and I had to restart the set-top box twice before I could watch TV programs.

The attitude of the service staff is positive, proactive and friendly. However, when checking in, the staff only gave one room card. This was very inconvenient. You need to express your wish to need two room cards with the front desk staff. Then he will give you another room card. Before traveling, you can ask the front desk to help you call a sightseeing battery car, but you need to wait for some time. You can take it wherever you want to go, and it is quite convenient to travel.

The absolute advantage here is that it has a large space and good air. It is really a pure natural oxygen bar! Especially after the rain, the air is fresh, and the temperature and humidity are just right these two days, making it comfortable.

Yiqin Garden at night is so quiet and comfortableüòåEnjoy the peace of mind away from the hustle and bustle of the city center!

The advantage of having a balcony is that you can hear the birds singing in the early morning, and you can also see a small bird nestling next to the big bird on the tree. From time to time, you poke your head out and look around. The ducks and ducks in the lake are happy and comfortable~~

This time there is still a D.I.Y. parent-child project, and we chose to make cookies this time. On a rainy day‚òîÔ∏èmaking cookies in the forest coffee bar feels very comfortable. Order a latte ‚òïÔ∏è, read a book and look at the scenery outside the window, without having to hang around the children, it‚Äôs so nice hahaha.

When the rain stopped, we walked slowly in the misty forest again. The birds were singing sweetly, and the withered yellow and tender green leaves that had been beaten by the rain were floating on the lake. It was such a wonderful time!

Remember, when you come here, don't pay too much attention to the facilities and equipment of the room, otherwise you will be disappointed.
